***tung.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a> (67042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tunge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tongue, language</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tungǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tongue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Liken <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zunge</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">tunga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dn̥ǵʰwéh₂s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tungs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Obsolete spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tongue</i></span></span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1557</b> July 16,  John Cheke,  “"Inkhorn" <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> John Cheke”, in  <cite>Univ of Victoria, Canada</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://internetshakespeare.uvic.ca/Library/SLT/literature/prose/cheke.html">[1]</a></sup>, retrieved <span class="mw-formatted-date" title="2012-09-29">2012-09-29</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I am of this opinion that our own <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></b> shold be written <a href = vnd.unilang:cleane.html>cleane</a> and pure, unmixt and unmangeled with borowing of other tunges, …</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1790</b>,  Noah Webster,  “The Founders' Constitution <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a> 1, Chap 15, <a href = vnd.unilang:doc.html>Doc</a> 44”, in  <cite>Univ. of Chicago</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://press-pubs.uchicago.edu/founders/documents/v1ch15s44.html">[2]</a></sup>, retrieved <span class="mw-formatted-date" title="2012-09-29">2012-09-29</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">… ever exposed to their envy, and the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></b> of slander …</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1832</b>,  Noah Webster, Edmund <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Barker,  <cite>A Dictionary of the English Language</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=YRdFAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA542amp;lpg=PA542amp;dq=%22Our+common+orthography+is+incorrect;+the+true+spelling+is+tung%22amp;source=blamp;ots=TCd0uQnNWOamp;sig=kaTfJywDsguD31NX0eB1sd_NOPcamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=w6BnUNTtEoOe8gS1pYDwBwamp;ved=0CF0Q6AEwCQ">[3]</a></sup>, Digitized edition, Black and Young, published <i>2010</i>, page 542:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Our common orthography <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incorrect; the true spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></b></i>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1848</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jonathan.html>Jonathan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgan.html>Morgan</a>,  <cite>The New <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a> of our Lord and Saviour Jesus Christ</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=66MsAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA215amp;lpg=PA215amp;dq=tungs+-Mao+-Tseamp;source=blamp;ots=npMIOWBVQAamp;sig=yM7XeQnYuUf8xaev7oImn9h32dEamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=UYdnUMulOI629gS01YDoCgamp;ved=0CE4Q6AEwBTgK">[4]</a></sup>, Digitized edition, SH Colesworthy, published <i>2008</i>, page 215:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">… <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> to be <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> with the understanding, that I may teach others also, than myriads of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tung.html>tung</a></b>. ... In the law, it hath <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> written, That, with other <b>tungs</b> and other <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a> I will speak to this people, and then they will not hear ...</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1872</b>,  Hugh Rowley,  <cite>Sage stuffing for green goslings; or, Saws for the goose and saws</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=jgkCAAAAQAAJamp;q=tungs+-Mao+-Tseamp;dq=tungs+-Mao+-Tseamp;source=blamp;ots=BuJadn-9B2amp;sig=8TsEjZLVGGOz25M6Cg9-fiq1zGUamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=j55nUKmaMeO_0QGPw4CADQamp;ved=0CFoQ6AEwCDh4">[5]</a></sup>, Digitized edition, published <i>2006</i>, page 159:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">If they've got anything to say which they want you to hear, let 'em say it out; if not, hold their <b>tungs</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>May be used by <a href = vnd.unilang:advocates.html>advocates</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English-language_spelling_reform" class="extiw" title="w:English-language spelling reform">English spelling reform</a>.
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tunieken.html>tunieken</a> (122548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tunieken.html>tunieken</a></strong>

***turkoois.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:turkoois.html>turkoois</a> (44483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:turquoise.html>Turquoise</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">(<a href = vnd.unilang:pierre.html>pierre</a>) turqueise</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Turkish (stone)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The stone <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> to Europe from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkestan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Turkestan">Turkestan</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:turkoois.html>turkoois</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:turkooizen.html>turkooizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:turkoois.html>turkooisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:turquoise.html>turquoise</a></span>, a gem <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (uncountable)</li>
<li>its typical, bright blue-greenish color <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (uncountable)
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:turkoois.html>turkoois</a> colour: <span style="background-color:40E0D0; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>

***tussen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> (398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tusschen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twisschen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tusschen</i>, a shortening of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">intwiskan</i>, originally a prepositional phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*in twiskan</i>. The latter word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twiskaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twiskijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twofold, double</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwís</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twice, doubly; in two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussentijd.html>tussentijd</a> (9253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">between</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***tutu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a> (42917)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cucu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bum, bottom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, playful reduplication of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cul</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tutus</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:ballet.html>ballet</a> skirt made of layered stiff but light netting.
<dl><dd><i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:ballet.html>ballet</a> dancer representing the swan wore a white <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/M%C4%81ori_language" class="extiw" title="w:Māori language">Maori</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tutus</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of the genus <i>Coriaria</i> of shrubs and trees found in New Zealand.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">toot plant</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tupakihi</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***twa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twa.html>twa</a> (25140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:twa.html>twa</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twai</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwóh₁</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_6">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:twa.html>twa</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>two</li></ol>
</body> 
***twaalf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twaalf.html>twaalf</a> (1457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twelef</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tweelf</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twalef</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twaelf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twelif</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twalif</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twalif</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zwölf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tolve</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twelve</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tolf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">tolv</i>.
</p>

***tweed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweed.html>tweed</a> (29578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span></span> tweel, with confusion with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/River_Tweed" class="extiw" title="w:River Tweed">River <a href = vnd.unilang:tweed.html>Tweed</a></a>, near which much cloth of this type <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> produced.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweed.html>tweed</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tweeds</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A coarse woolen fabric used for clothing.

He wore a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tweed.html>tweed</a></b> suit, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>, I think.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two, bi-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dek.html>dek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deck, plane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

***tweeling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a> (3366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twiling</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twilling</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tweiling</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twinling</i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twinilingaz</i>, with the first element from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twinaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zwilling</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twinling</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tvilling</i>); or a more recent formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweelingen.html>tweelingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweelingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pair of twins; <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of people and other mammals.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My brother and I are <b>twins</b>.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">My brother and I are a <b>twin [pair]</b>.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">less common, usually plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Each of two twin siblings.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>twin</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never alone.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A vegetal or object equivalent, e.g. an identical fruit pair</li></ol>

***tweelingbroer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweelingbroer.html>tweelingbroer</a> (13892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijd.html>strijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">battle, struggle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twijfel.html>twijfel</a> (1838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twivel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twifel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">twīval</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twīflaz</i>, an old derivation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfel.html>twijfel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfels.html>twijfels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfel.html>twijfeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">doubt</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">uncertainty</span></li></ol>

***twijfelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaar</a> (67022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twivelaer</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelen.html>twijfelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaars.html>twijfelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A doubter, hesitater; one who doubts or hesitates.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> of a size that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in between those of a regular single size <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> and a double <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>, typically with a breadth of 120 or 140 centimetres.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaar</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelt.html>twijfelt</a></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twintich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twēntig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twai tigiwiz</i>.
